# Documentation Exception Disposition Inventory

## Integrity Header

- Inventory entries: 573.
- Baseline entries: 573.
- Exception entries: 573.
- Path sets equal: true.
- Sorted path-set SHA-256: `9e2426c0a872ce9d1257a39c273399eea3acde49a9b80a7543020a2c649b542d`.
- Method: deterministic path-domain partition using registry metadata only.
- Document bodies or sensitive values inspected or copied: no.

## Rules

- `docs/**` → `MIGRATE`; individual ADR-018/019 gates remain mandatory.
- `.knowledge/**` → `AUTHORITY_REVIEW`; location cannot establish authority.
- `.instructions/**` → `SECURITY_REVIEW`; evidence remains isolated and redacted.
- Other/historical paths → `DEFER_WITH_RISK`; retention and authority require review.
- Every row is P0 because the current exception expires on 2026-10-01 without an applied successor decision.
- Security routing is conservative category evidence, not a secret finding.

This request inventoried and classified remaining exception dispositions only. It did not migrate legacy documents, promote canonical documents from legacy sources, reserve final IDs, remove or mutate baseline entries, remove or mutate exception registry entries, enable production, execute financial actions, use credentials, enable providers, write contracts, modify production databases or open operational gates.
